CPDN REST API API documentation version v1

https://api.cpdn.sd2.cz/v1

/schemes

Scheme root resource

/schemes get post

get

Get a list of schemes.

post

Add a new scheme.

get /schemes

Get a list of schemes.

Secured by oauth_2_0

OAuth 2.0 for authenticating all API requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • e: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to expand field of the collection or the collection item. Use it only if you want expand any element from available expandable elements in current scope. General example: (calc,section.spec, ...)

    Example:

    (scheme)
  • s: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to sort the results. By default, the column values are sorted in ascending order. Can either be in the form of fieldName or fieldName:asc.

    Example:

    (id,description,name,version,lock,tsCreate,tsUpdate)
  • q: (string)

    The list of semicolon-separated properties used to filter the collection. Use it only if you want filter the collection for selected parameters. Some collections may have required parameters in filter query. These parameters are with leading ! in example doc. General example: (color=blue;wheels=15; ...) Required param: (!color=blue)

    Example:

    (description=string;name=string;version=int,lock=string-bool)
  • pageNumber: (integer - default: 1)

    Page number. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    1
  • pageSize: (integer - default: 25)

    Page size. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    25

HTTP status code 200

Body

Type: application/json

Example:

{
    "_meta": {
        "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/schemes\/",
        "mediaType": "application\/json"
    },
    "items": [
        {
            "_meta": {
                "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/schemes\/44\/",
                "mediaType": "application\/json",
                "id": 44
            }
        },
        {
            "_meta": {
                "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/schemes\/44\/",
                "mediaType": "application\/json",
                "id": 44
            }
        },
        {
            "_meta": {
                "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/schemes\/44\/",
                "mediaType": "application\/json",
                "id": 44
            }
        }
    ],
    "pageNumber": 1,
    "pageSize": 25,
    "itemsTotal": 100,
    "pagesTotal": 4,
    "first": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/schemes\/?pageNumber=1&pageSize=25",
            "mediaType": "application\/json"
        }
    },
    "previous": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/schemes\/?pageNumber=1&pageSize=25",
            "mediaType": "application\/json"
        }
    },
    "next": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/schemes\/?pageNumber=2&pageSize=25",
            "mediaType": "application\/json"
        }
    },
    "last": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/schemes\/?pageNumber=4&pageSize=25",
            "mediaType": "application\/json"
        }
    }
}

Read/update/delete entity representing a scheme

get

Get the collection item of scheme

post

Update the collection item of scheme

delete

Delete the collection item of scheme

get /schemes/{scheme_id}

Secured by oauth_2_0

OAuth 2.0 for authenticating all API requests.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • scheme_id: required (string)

Query Parameters

    The list of comma-separated properties used to expand field of the collection or the collection item. Use it only if you want expand any element from available expandable elements in current scope. General example: (calc,section.spec, ...)

    Example:

    ()

/schemes/{scheme_id}/nodes get

Read collection of nodes.

get

Get a list of nodes.

get /schemes/{scheme_id}/nodes

Get a list of nodes.

Secured by oauth_2_0

OAuth 2.0 for authenticating all API requests.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • scheme_id: required (string)

Query Parameters

  • e: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to expand field of the collection or the collection item. Use it only if you want expand any element from available expandable elements in current scope. General example: (calc,section.spec, ...)

    Example:

    (node,node.calc,node.mapPoint,node.spec)
  • s: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to sort the results. By default, the column values are sorted in ascending order. Can either be in the form of fieldName or fieldName:asc.

    Example:

    (id,schemeId,mapPointId,tsCreate,tsUpdate)
  • q: (string)

    The list of semicolon-separated properties used to filter the collection. Use it only if you want filter the collection for selected parameters. Some collections may have required parameters in filter query. These parameters are with leading ! in example doc. General example: (color=blue;wheels=15; ...) Required param: (!color=blue)

    Example:

    ()
  • pageNumber: (integer - default: 1)

    Page number. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    1
  • pageSize: (integer - default: 25)

    Page size. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    25

HTTP status code 200

Body

Type: application/json

Example:

{
    "_meta": {
        "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/schemes\/44\/nodes\/",
        "mediaType": "application\/json"
    },
    "items": [
        {
            "_meta": {
                "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/nodes\/22\/",
                "mediaType": "application\/json",
                "id": 22
            }
        },
        {
            "_meta": {
                "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/nodes\/22\/",
                "mediaType": "application\/json",
                "id": 22
            }
        }
    ],
    "pageNumber": 1,
    "pageSize": 25,
    "itemsTotal": 100,
    "pagesTotal": 4,
    "first": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/schemes\/44\/nodes\/?pageNumber=1&pageSize=25",
            "mediaType": "application\/json"
        }
    },
    "previous": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/schemes\/44\/nodes\/?pageNumber=1&pageSize=25",

/schemes/{scheme_id}/sections get

Read collection of sections.

get

Get a list of sections.

get /schemes/{scheme_id}/sections

Get a list of sections.

Secured by oauth_2_0

OAuth 2.0 for authenticating all API requests.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • scheme_id: required (string)

Query Parameters

  • e: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to expand field of the collection or the collection item. Use it only if you want expand any element from available expandable elements in current scope. General example: (calc,section.spec, ...)

    Example:

    (section,section.calc,section.nodes,section.spec)
  • s: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to sort the results. By default, the column values are sorted in ascending order. Can either be in the form of fieldName or fieldName:asc.

    Example:

    (id,schemeId,tsCreate,tsUpdate)
  • q: (string)

    The list of semicolon-separated properties used to filter the collection. Use it only if you want filter the collection for selected parameters. Some collections may have required parameters in filter query. These parameters are with leading ! in example doc. General example: (color=blue;wheels=15; ...) Required param: (!color=blue)

    Example:

    (!schemeId=int)
  • pageNumber: (integer - default: 1)

    Page number. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    1
  • pageSize: (integer - default: 25)

    Page size. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    25

    Example:

    (id,schemeId,gpsLatitude,gpsLongitude,gpsAltitude,nodeId,schemeId,x,y,tsCreate,tsUpdate)

/schemes/{scheme_id}/tasks get

Read collection of tasks.

get

Get a list of tasks.

get /schemes/{scheme_id}/tasks

Get a list of tasks.

Secured by oauth_2_0

OAuth 2.0 for authenticating all API requests.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • scheme_id: required (string)

Query Parameters

  • e: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to expand field of the collection or the collection item. Use it only if you want expand any element from available expandable elements in current scope. General example: (calc,section.spec, ...)

    Example:

    (task,task.user,task.executor,task.scheme)
  • s: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to sort the results. By default, the column values are sorted in ascending order. Can either be in the form of fieldName or fieldName:asc.

    Example:

    (id,schemeId,profileId,executorId,status,priority,command,result,tsCreate,tsUpdate,tsRtsReceive,tsExecute)
  • q: (string)

    The list of semicolon-separated properties used to filter the collection. Use it only if you want filter the collection for selected parameters. Some collections may have required parameters in filter query. These parameters are with leading ! in example doc. General example: (color=blue;wheels=15; ...) Required param: (!color=blue)

    Example:

    (!schemeId=int;profileId=int;executorId=int;status=string;priority=int;command=string;result=string;tsCreate=tsUpdate=tsRtsReceive=tsExecute=string timestamp)
  • pageNumber: (integer - default: 1)

    Page number. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    1
  • pageSize: (integer - default: 25)

    Page size. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    25

/sections

Section root resource

/sections get post

get

Get a list of sections.

post

Add a new section.

get /sections

Get a list of sections.

Secured by oauth_2_0

OAuth 2.0 for authenticating all API requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • e: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to expand field of the collection or the collection item. Use it only if you want expand any element from available expandable elements in current scope. General example: (calc,section.spec, ...)

    Example:

    (section,section.calc,section.nodes,section.scheme,section.spec)
  • s: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to sort the results. By default, the column values are sorted in ascending order. Can either be in the form of fieldName or fieldName:asc.

    Example:

    (id,schemeId,tsCreate,tsUpdate)
  • q: (string)

    The list of semicolon-separated properties used to filter the collection. Use it only if you want filter the collection for selected parameters. Some collections may have required parameters in filter query. These parameters are with leading ! in example doc. General example: (color=blue;wheels=15; ...) Required param: (!color=blue)

    Example:

    (!schemeId=int)
  • pageNumber: (integer - default: 1)

    Page number. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    1
  • pageSize: (integer - default: 25)

    Page size. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    25

HTTP status code 200

Body

Type: application/json

Example:

{
    "_meta": {
        "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/sections\/",
        "mediaType": "application\/json"

                "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/sections\/33\/",

delete

get /sections/{section_id}

Get the collection item of section

Secured by oauth_2_0

OAuth 2.0 for authenticating all API requests.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • section_id: required (string)

Query Parameters

  • e: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to expand field of the collection or the collection item. Use it only if you want expand any element from available expandable elements in current scope. General example: (calc,section.spec, ...)

    Example:

    (calc,nodes,scheme,spec)

/sections/{section_id}/paths get

Read collection of paths.

get

Get a list of paths.

get /sections/{section_id}/paths

Get a list of paths.

Secured by oauth_2_0

OAuth 2.0 for authenticating all API requests.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • section_id: required (string)

Query Parameters

  • e: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to expand field of the collection or the collection item. Use it only if you want expand any element from available expandable elements in current scope. General example: (calc,section.spec, ...)

    Example:

    (path,path.mapPoint.dst,path.mapPoint.src)
  • s: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to sort the results. By default, the column values are sorted in ascending order. Can either be in the form of fieldName or fieldName:asc.

    Example:

    (mapPoint.src,mapPoint.dst)
  • q: (string)

    The list of semicolon-separated properties used to filter the collection. Use it only if you want filter the collection for selected parameters. Some collections may have required parameters in filter query. These parameters are with leading ! in example doc. General example: (color=blue;wheels=15; ...) Required param: (!color=blue)

    Example:

    (srcMapPoint=int;dstMapPoint=int)
  • pageNumber: (integer - default: 1)

    Page number. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    1
  • pageSize: (integer - default: 25)

    Page size. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    25

Body

Type: application/json

Example:

/mapPoints

MapPoint root resource

/mapPoints get post

get

Get a list of mapPoints.

post

Add a new mapPoint.

get /mapPoints

Get a list of mapPoints.

Secured by oauth_2_0

OAuth 2.0 for authenticating all API requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • e: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to expand field of the collection or the collection item. Use it only if you want expand any element from available expandable elements in current scope. General example: (calc,section.spec, ...)

    Example:

    (mapPoint,mapPoint.node,mapPoint.scheme)
  • s: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to sort the results. By default, the column values are sorted in ascending order. Can either be in the form of fieldName or fieldName:asc.

    Example:

    (id,schemeId,gpsLatitude,gpsLongitude,gpsAltitude,nodeId,schemeId,x,y,tsCreate,tsUpdate)
  • q: (string)

    The list of semicolon-separated properties used to filter the collection. Use it only if you want filter the collection for selected parameters. Some collections may have required parameters in filter query. These parameters are with leading ! in example doc. General example: (color=blue;wheels=15; ...) Required param: (!color=blue)

    Example:

    (!schemeId=int;gpsLatitude=double;gpsLongitude=double;gpsAltitude=double;nodeId=int;x=double;y=double)
  • pageNumber: (integer - default: 1)

    Page number. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    1
  • pageSize: (integer - default: 25)

    Page size. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    25

HTTP status code 200

Body

Type: application/json

/paths

Path root resource

/paths get post

get

Get a list of paths.

post

Add a new path.

get /paths

Get a list of paths.

Secured by oauth_2_0

OAuth 2.0 for authenticating all API requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • e: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to expand field of the collection or the collection item. Use it only if you want expand any element from available expandable elements in current scope. General example: (calc,section.spec, ...)

    Example:

    (path,path.mapPoint.dst,path.mapPoint.src,path.section)
  • s: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to sort the results. By default, the column values are sorted in ascending order. Can either be in the form of fieldName or fieldName:asc.

    Example:

    (id,sectionId,srcMapPointId,dstMapPointId,tsCreate,tsUpdate)
  • q: (string)

    The list of semicolon-separated properties used to filter the collection. Use it only if you want filter the collection for selected parameters. Some collections may have required parameters in filter query. These parameters are with leading ! in example doc. General example: (color=blue;wheels=15; ...) Required param: (!color=blue)

    Example:

    (!sectionId=int;srcMapPointId=int;dstMapPointId=int)
  • pageNumber: (integer - default: 1)

    Page number. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    1
  • pageSize: (integer - default: 25)

    Page size. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    25

HTTP status code 200

Body

Type: application/json

Example:

{
    "_meta": {
        "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/paths\/",

/objects

Object root resource

/objects get post

get

Get a list of objects.

post

Add a new object.

get /objects

Get a list of objects.

Secured by oauth_2_0

OAuth 2.0 for authenticating all API requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • e: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to expand field of the collection or the collection item. Use it only if you want expand any element from available expandable elements in current scope. General example: (calc,section.spec, ...)

    Example:

    (object,object.scheme)
  • s: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to sort the results. By default, the column values are sorted in ascending order. Can either be in the form of fieldName or fieldName:asc.

    Example:

    (id,scheme,name,tsCreate,tsUpdate)
  • q: (string)

    The list of semicolon-separated properties used to filter the collection. Use it only if you want filter the collection for selected parameters. Some collections may have required parameters in filter query. These parameters are with leading ! in example doc. General example: (color=blue;wheels=15; ...) Required param: (!color=blue)

    Example:

    (!schemeId=int;name=string)
  • pageNumber: (integer - default: 1)

    Page number. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    1
  • pageSize: (integer - default: 25)

    Page size. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    25

HTTP status code 200

Body

Type: application/json

Example:

{
    "_meta": {
        "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/objects\/",
        "mediaType": "application\/json"
    },
    "items": [
        {
            "_meta": {
                "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/objects\/99\/",
                "mediaType": "application\/json",
                "id": 99
            }
        },
        {
            "_meta": {
                "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/objects\/99\/",
                "mediaType": "application\/json",
                "id": 99
            }
        }
    ],
    "pageNumber": 1,
    "pageSize": 25,
    "itemsTotal": 100,
    "pagesTotal": 4,
    "first": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/objects\/?pageNumber=1&pageSize=25",
            "mediaType": "application\/json"
        }
    },
    "previous": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/objects\/?pageNumber=1&pageSize=25",
            "mediaType": "application\/json"
        }
    },
    "next": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/objects\/?pageNumber=2&pageSize=25",
            "mediaType": "application\/json"
        }
    },
    "last": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/objects\/?pageNumber=4&pageSize=25",
            "mediaType": "application\/json"
        }
    }
}

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • object_id: required (string)

Query Parameters

  • e: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to expand field of the collection or the collection item. Use it only if you want expand any element from available expandable elements in current scope. General example: (calc,section.spec, ...)

    Example:

    ()
  • s: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to sort the results. By default, the column values are sorted in ascending order. Can either be in the form of fieldName or fieldName:asc.

    Example:

    ()
  • q: (string)

    The list of semicolon-separated properties used to filter the collection. Use it only if you want filter the collection for selected parameters. Some collections may have required parameters in filter query. These parameters are with leading ! in example doc. General example: (color=blue;wheels=15; ...) Required param: (!color=blue)

    Example:

    ()
  • pageNumber: (integer - default: 1)

    Page number. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

  • pageSize: (integer - default: 25)

    Page size. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    25

/notifications

Notification root resource

/notifications get

get

Get a list of notifications.

get /notifications

Get a list of notifications.

Secured by oauth_2_0

OAuth 2.0 for authenticating all API requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • e: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to expand field of the collection or the collection item. Use it only if you want expand any element from available expandable elements in current scope. General example: (calc,section.spec, ...)

    Example:

    (notification,notification.user)
  • s: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to sort the results. By default, the column values are sorted in ascending order. Can either be in the form of fieldName or fieldName:asc.

    Example:

    (id,profileId,title,content,tsCreate,tsUpdate,tsRead)
  • q: (string)

    The list of semicolon-separated properties used to filter the collection. Use it only if you want filter the collection for selected parameters. Some collections may have required parameters in filter query. These parameters are with leading ! in example doc. General example: (color=blue;wheels=15; ...) Required param: (!color=blue)

    Example:

    (!profileId=int;title=string;content=string;tsCreate=string-time;tsRead=string-time)
  • pageNumber: (integer - default: 1)

    Page number. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    1
  • pageSize: (integer - default: 25)

    Page size. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    25

/permissions

Permission root resource

/permissions get post

get

Get a list of permissions.

post

Add a new permission.

get /permissions

Get a list of permissions.

Secured by oauth_2_0

OAuth 2.0 for authenticating all API requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • e: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to expand field of the collection or the collection item. Use it only if you want expand any element from available expandable elements in current scope. General example: (calc,section.spec, ...)

    Example:

    (permission,permission.user,permission.scheme,permission.executor)
  • s: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to sort the results. By default, the column values are sorted in ascending order. Can either be in the form of fieldName or fieldName:asc.

    Example:

    (id,schemeId,profileId,mode,tsFrom,tsTo)
  • q: (string)

    The list of semicolon-separated properties used to filter the collection. Use it only if you want filter the collection for selected parameters. Some collections may have required parameters in filter query. These parameters are with leading ! in example doc. General example: (color=blue;wheels=15; ...) Required param: (!color=blue)

    Example:

    (schemeId=int;profileId=int;mode=string;tsFrom=string-time;tsTo=string-time)
  • pageNumber: (integer - default: 1)

    Page number. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    1
  • pageSize: (integer - default: 25)

    Page size. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    25

HTTP status code 200

Body

Type: application/json

Example:

{
    "_meta": {
        "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/permissions\/77\/",
        "mediaType": "application\/json",
        "id": 77,
        "tsCreate": "2015-01-01T00:00:00.000Z",
        "tsUpdate": "2015-01-01T00:00:00.000Z"
    },
    "user": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/users\/7\/",

            "id": 7
        }
    },
    "scheme": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/schemes\/44\/",

        }
    },
    "mode": "rwx",
    "tsFrom": "2015-01-01T00:00:00.000Z",

post

Add a new task.

get /tasks

Get a list of tasks.

Secured by oauth_2_0

OAuth 2.0 for authenticating all API requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • e: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to expand field of the collection or the collection item. Use it only if you want expand any element from available expandable elements in current scope. General example: (calc,section.spec, ...)

    Example:

    (task,task.user,task.executor,task.scheme)
  • s: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to sort the results. By default, the column values are sorted in ascending order. Can either be in the form of fieldName or fieldName:asc.

    Example:

    (id,schemeId,profileId,executorId,status,priority,command,result,tsCreate,tsUpdate,tsRtsReceive,tsExecute)
  • q: (string)

    The list of semicolon-separated properties used to filter the collection. Use it only if you want filter the collection for selected parameters. Some collections may have required parameters in filter query. These parameters are with leading ! in example doc. General example: (color=blue;wheels=15; ...) Required param: (!color=blue)

    Example:

    (schemeId=int;profileId=int;executorId=int;status=string;priority=int;command=string;result=string;tsCreate=tsUpdate=tsRtsReceive=tsExecute=string timestamp)
  • pageNumber: (integer - default: 1)

    Page number. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    1
  • pageSize: (integer - default: 25)

    Page size. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    25

HTTP status code 200

Body

Type: application/json

Example:

{
    "_meta": {
        "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/tasks\/",
        "mediaType": "application\/json"
    },
    "items": [
        {
            "_meta": {
                "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/tasks\/88\/",
                "mediaType": "application\/json",
                "id": 88
            }
        },
        {
            "_meta": {
                "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/tasks\/88\/",
                "mediaType": "application\/json",
                "id": 88
            }
        }
    ],
    "pageNumber": 1,
    "pageSize": 25,
    "itemsTotal": 100,
    "pagesTotal": 4,
    "first": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/tasks\/?pageNumber=1&pageSize=25",
            "mediaType": "application\/json"
        }
    },
    "previous": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/tasks\/?pageNumber=1&pageSize=25",
            "mediaType": "application\/json"
        }
    },
    "next": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/tasks\/?pageNumber=2&pageSize=25",
            "mediaType": "application\/json"
        }
    },
    "last": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/tasks\/?pageNumber=4&pageSize=25",
            "mediaType": "application\/json"
        }
    }
}

  • Response

Type: application/json

Example:

    "user": 7,
    "executor": null,
    "scheme": 44,
    "status": "new",
    "priority": 1,
    "command": "{json:encoded:command:to:executor}",
    "result": "{json:encoded:result:from:executor}"
}

/tasks/{task_id} get post

Read/update entity representing a task

get

Get the collection item of task

post

Update the collection item of task

get /tasks/{task_id}

Get the collection item of task

Secured by oauth_2_0

OAuth 2.0 for authenticating all API requests.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • task_id: required (string)

Query Parameters

  • e: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to expand field of the collection or the collection item. Use it only if you want expand any element from available expandable elements in current scope. General example: (calc,section.spec, ...)

    Example:

    (user,executor,scheme)

HTTP status code 200

Body

Type: application/json

Example:

{
    "_meta": {
        "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/tasks\/88\/",
        "mediaType": "application\/json",
        "id": 88,
        "tsCreate": "2015-01-01T00:00:00.000Z",
        "tsUpdate": "2015-01-01T00:00:00.000Z"
    },
    "user": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/users\/7\/",
            "mediaType": "application\/json",
            "id": 7
        }
    },
    "executor": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/executors\/222\/",
            "mediaType": "application\/json",
            "id": 222
        }
    },
    "scheme": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/schemes\/44\/",
            "mediaType": "application\/json",
            "id": 44
        }
    },
    "status": "new",
    "priority": 1,
    "command": "{json:encoded:command:to:executor}",
    "result": "{json:encoded:result:from:executor}",
    "tsReceived": "2015-01-01T00:00:00.000Z",
    "tsExecuted": "2015-01-01T00:00:00.000Z"
}

/executors

Executor root resource

get

Get a list of executors.

OAuth 2.0 for authenticating all API requests.

  • Response

Query Parameters

/users

User root resource

/users get

get

Get a list of users.

get /users

Get a list of users.

Secured by oauth_2_0

OAuth 2.0 for authenticating all API requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • e: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to expand field of the collection or the collection item. Use it only if you want expand any element from available expandable elements in current scope. General example: (calc,section.spec, ...)

    Example:

    (user)
  • s: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to sort the results. By default, the column values are sorted in ascending order. Can either be in the form of fieldName or fieldName:asc.

    Example:

    (id,tsCreate,tsUpdate,nick)
  • q: (string)

    The list of semicolon-separated properties used to filter the collection. Use it only if you want filter the collection for selected parameters. Some collections may have required parameters in filter query. These parameters are with leading ! in example doc. General example: (color=blue;wheels=15; ...) Required param: (!color=blue)

    Example:

    (id=int;nick=string)
  • pageNumber: (integer - default: 1)

    Page number. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    1
  • pageSize: (integer - default: 25)

    Page size. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    25

HTTP status code 200

Body

Type: application/json

Example:

{
    "_meta": {
        "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/users\/",
        "mediaType": "application\/json"

        {

    "pageSize": 25,
    "itemsTotal": 100,
    "pagesTotal": 4,
    "first": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/users\/?pageNumber=1&pageSize=25",
            "mediaType": "application\/json"
        }
    },
    "previous": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/users\/?pageNumber=1&pageSize=25",
            "mediaType": "application\/json"
        }
    },
    "next": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/users\/?pageNumber=2&pageSize=25",
            "mediaType": "application\/json"
        }
    },
    "last": {
        "_meta": {
            "href": "https:\/\/api.cpdn.sd2.cz\/v1\/users\/?pageNumber=4&pageSize=25",

/configs/idp get

IdP config root resource

get

Get a list of idp.

get /configs/idp

Get a list of idp.

Secured by oauth_2_0

OAuth 2.0 for authenticating all API requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • e: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to expand field of the collection or the collection item. Use it only if you want expand any element from available expandable elements in current scope. General example: (calc,section.spec, ...)

    Example:

    (config)
  • s: (string)

    The list of comma-separated properties used to sort the results. By default, the column values are sorted in ascending order. Can either be in the form of fieldName or fieldName:asc.

    Example:

    (key=string;value=string)
  • q: (string)

    The list of semicolon-separated properties used to filter the collection. Use it only if you want filter the collection for selected parameters. Some collections may have required parameters in filter query. These parameters are with leading ! in example doc. General example: (color=blue;wheels=15; ...) Required param: (!color=blue)

    Example:

    ()
  • pageNumber: (integer - default: 1)

    Page number. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    1
  • pageSize: (integer - default: 25)

    Page size. If you want select all items from collection without paged feature, DO NOT USE this query parameter.

    Example:

    25
